%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%-8.22计算每列的信息-熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%-
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%把data_312_   替换成train_data1_  ,再把data_312 替换成train_data1

train_data1_1lie=train_data1(:,1)
train_data1_1liezhongleixing=unique(train_data1_1lie)

hanglietrain_data1_1lie= size(train_data1_1liezhongleixing)
hangshutrain_data1_1lie=hanglietrain_data1_1lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data1_1lie=hanglietrain_data1_1lie(1,2)



hanglietrain_data1= size(train_data1)
train_data1_hangshu=hanglietrain_data1(1,1)
train_data1_lieshu=hanglietrain_data1(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data1_1lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
     j=0;
    for i=1:train_data1_hangshu
        if train_data1(i,1) == train_data1_1liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data1_1lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data1_1lie' %%转置
result_train_data1_1lie = [train_data1_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_1lie'];

train_data1_1lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
       train_data1_1lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data1_1lie(m)/train_data1_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data1_1lie = [train_data1_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_1lie',train_data1_1lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data1_1lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data1_sumshang1= 0;
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
       train_data1_1lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data1_1lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data1_1lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data1_sumshang1= train_data1_sumshang1+  train_data1_1lie_xinxishang(m);
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%   traindata1的第2列数据的信息熵 

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出 traindata1的第2列的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

train_data1_2lie=train_data1(:,2)
train_data1_2liezhongleixing=unique(train_data1_2lie)


hanglietrain_data1_2lie= size(train_data1_2liezhongleixing)

lieshutrain_data1_2lie=hanglietrain_data1_2lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data1_2lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_2lie
     j=0;
    for i=1:train_data1_hangshu
        if train_data1(i,2) == train_data1_2liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data1_2lie(m)=j;;
    end
end

arr_train_data1_2lie' %%转置
result_train_data1_2lie = [train_data1_2liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_2lie'];

train_data1_2lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_2lie
       train_data1_2lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data1_2lie(m)/train_data1_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data1_2lie = [train_data1_2liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_2lie',train_data1_2lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data1_2lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data1_sumshang2 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_2lie
       train_data1_2lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data1_2lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data1_2lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data1_sumshang2 = train_data1_sumshang2 +  train_data1_2lie_xinxishang(m);

lieshutrain_data1_13lie=hanglietrain_data1_13lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data1_13lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_13lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data1_hangshu
        if train_data1(i,13) == train_data1_13liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data1_13lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data1_13lie' %%转置
result_train_data1_13lie = [train_data1_13liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_13lie'];

train_data1_13lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_13lie
       train_data1_13lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data1_13lie(m)/train_data1_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data1_13lie = [train_data1_13liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_13lie',train_data1_13lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data1_13lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data1_sumshang13 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_13lie
       train_data1_13lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data1_13lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data1_13lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data1_sumshang13 = train_data1_sumshang13 +  train_data1_13lie_xinxishang(m);
end

hangshutrain_data2_9lie=hanglietrain_data2_9lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data2_9lie=hanglietrain_data2_9lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data2_9lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_9lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data2_hangshu
        if train_data2(i,9) == train_data2_9liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data2_9lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data2_9lie' %%转置
result_train_data2_9lie = [train_data2_9liezhongleixing,arr_train_data2_9lie'];

train_data2_9lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_9lie
       train_data2_9lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data2_9lie(m)/train_data2_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data2_9lie = [train_data2_9liezhongleixing,arr_train_data2_9lie',train_data2_9lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data2_9lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data2_sumshang9 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_9lie
       train_data2_9lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data2_9lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data2_9lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data2_sumshang9 = train_data2_sumshang9 +  train_data2_9lie_xinxishang(m);
end

     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data2_hangshu
        if train_data2(i,34) == train_data2_34liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data2_34lie(m)=j;
    end

       train_data2_34lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data2_34lie(m)/train_data2_hangshu;
end

       train_data2_34lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data2_34lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data2_34lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data2_sumshang34 = train_data2_sumshang34 +  train_data2_34lie_xinxishang(m);

hangshutrain_data3_5lie=hanglietrain_data3_5lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data3_5lie=hanglietrain_data3_5lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data3_5lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_5lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data3_hangshu
        if train_data3(i,5) == train_data3_5liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data3_5lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data3_5lie' %%转置
result_train_data3_5lie = [train_data3_5liezhongleixing,arr_train_data3_5lie'];

train_data3_5lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_5lie
       train_data3_5lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data3_5lie(m)/train_data3_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data3_5lie = [train_data3_5liezhongleixing,arr_train_data3_5lie',train_data3_5lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data3_5lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data3_sumshang5 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_5lie
       train_data3_5lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data3_5lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data3_5lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data3_sumshang5 = train_data3_sumshang5 +  train_data3_5lie_xinxishang(m);
end

       train_data3_sumshang29 = train_data3_sumshang29 +  train_data3_29lie_xinxishang(m);
end

hanglietrain_data4= size(train_data4)
train_data4_hangshu=hanglietrain_data4(1,1)
train_data4_lieshu=hanglietrain_data4(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data4_1lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_1lie
     j=0;
    for i=1:train_data4_hangshu
        if train_data4(i,1) == train_data4_1liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data4_1lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data4_1lie' %%转置
result_train_data4_1lie = [train_data4_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data4_1lie'];

train_data4_1lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_1lie
       train_data4_1lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data4_1lie(m)/train_data4_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data4_1lie = [train_data4_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data4_1lie',train_data4_1lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data4_1lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data4_sumshang1= 0;
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_1lie
       train_data4_1lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data4_1lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data4_1lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data4_sumshang1= train_data4_sumshang1+  train_data4_1lie_xinxishang(m);
end

for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_38lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data4_hangshu
        if train_data4(i,38) == train_data4_38liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data4_38lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data4_38lie' %%转置

train_data4_38lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_38lie
       train_data4_38lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data4_38lie(m)/train_data4_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data4_38lie = [train_data4_38liezhongleixing,arr_train_data4_38lie',train_data4_38lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data4_38lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data4_sumshang38 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_38lie
       train_data4_38lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data4_38lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data4_38lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data4_sumshang38 = train_data4_sumshang38 +  train_data4_38lie_xinxishang(m);
end

for m=1: hangshutrain_data5_34lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data5_hangshu
        if train_data5(i,34) == train_data5_34liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data5_34lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data5_34lie' %%转置
result_train_data5_34lie = [train_data5_34liezhongleixing,arr_train_data5_34lie'];

train_data5_34lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data5_34lie
       train_data5_34lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data5_34lie(m)/train_data5_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data5_34lie = [train_data5_34liezhongleixing,arr_train_data5_34lie',train_data5_34lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data5_34lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data5_sumshang34 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data5_34lie
       train_data5_34lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data5_34lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data5_34lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data5_sumshang34 = train_data5_sumshang34 +  train_data5_34lie_xinxishang(m);
end
